3a1(1): nas khyang rgyal ba bcag pa dngam/ bdag sa chanags/ na dan papas kyi
3a2(1): smras pa/ jiltar khyod kyi grogs bram ze 'i yab kyi mdun na 'don du bcug pa de bzhin khyod kyang nga'i
3a3(1): mdun na 'don du gzhug go zhes byas pa'i gtam de gcig nas gcig tu rgyud de/ bram ze mdun na 'don
3a4(1): des thos nas/ de'ongasnyam du semos te/ ngas ci nas gzhon nu nyid kyis kyang rgyal srid mi thob pa de lta
3b1(1): byan/ mdun na 'don du zhugs pa lta smos kyang ci dgos snyam mo/ ci tsam dus gzhan nigan rgyal po de'i yul nar
3b2(1): 'or ba zhig sngo bar gyur nas/ rgyal pos de 'bebs su dmag kha cen cig btang nas/ de bcom rnam par bcom ste/ pham
3b3(1): par byas nas slar log go// de bzhin du kha cen bdun gyi bang btang ba las/ de rnams kyang bcom rnam par bcom ste/ 
3b4(1): pham par byas nas la slar lpags so// rgyal po chen po rnams la blon po rnams kyis gsol pa/ lha ci'i slad durang dpung
3b5(1): nyams shing gzhan gyi mthu bskyed par mdzad/ gang yang lha'i yul na mtshon gyis 'tsho ba ji snyed mchis pa thams cad dgu gi du gsol
4a1(1): brab ze mdun da 'don gyis bsams pa/ gzhon nu gas pa'i thabs bya ba'i dus 'di la
4a2(1): desnyam nas/ des rgyal po la gsol pa/ lha de lta bus ni dbab par rngo ma thogs/ rgyal pos smras pa/ ji ltar bya
4a3(1): nyid kho na 'gro'am/ mdun na 'don gyis smras pa/ ci'i slad du lta nyid gshegs/ gzhon na nor bzangs 'di ni/ 
4a4(1): dngal bab cing mthu rtsal bsnyems pa dang ldan pa legs pas/ dmags 'di rnams dang ldan cig dbyer gsol/ rgyal/ 
4b1(1): pos smras pa/ de bzhin du bya'o// zhes de nas rgyal pos gnon nu bka/ ga nas bsgo ba/ gnon nu dmag dang ldan cig tu de la ra'ang
4b2(1): brnams pob shig/ lha bka' bzhin 'aral zhes gnon nu nor bzangs kyis rnal po las nyan nas/ btsun mo rnams kyi nang du
4b3(1): song ste/ yid 'phrog ma mthong ba dang / des thams cad brjed par gyur to// de nas yang rgyal pos bsgo ba dang / yang dam
4b4(1): thag tu thams cad brjed par gyur to// de nas mdun 'dod gyis rgyal po la smras pa/ lha gzhon nu nor bzangs ni yid 'phrog ma la lhag
4b5(1): par chags pas mchi rje ma grig gi dmag sngags la/ gzhon nu btsun mo rnams kyi nang nas byung ba dang tsa nas kyang yad
5a1(1): 'phrog ma'i drung dum 'gro bar thal byung ba dang bar brgya'o// rgyal pos blon po rnams la smras pa/ 
5a2(1): shoso ldan dag dpung gi tshogs sta gon gyis shi ga blon po rnams kyis rgyal po las mnyan nas dpung gi tshogs glang po che dang / rta dang dang
5a3(1): bu rung phrin sum tshogs pa/ tshogs chas go mtshon rnam pa du ma dang ldan pa dag sta gon byas so// de ras gnod nu phyir byed pa dang / sgo ba gzhan/ 
5a4(1): nu dpung gi tshogs sta gor byas kyi song shig des smras pa/ lha yid 'phrog la bltas te mchi bar bgyi'o// rgyal pos spros pa gzhon nu thogs par
5a5(1): 'gyur gyis ma blta zhig/ yab gal te de lta na maM la ltas te mchi'o// gzhon nu ma la ltos shig/ des yid 'phrog ma'o gtsug gi ni jo bu khyer
5a6(1): nas ma 'drung du sadziH/ gang pa gnyis la gtags smras pa/ yum bdag ring ba rnams 'bebs su mchis lags kyis/ gtsug gnor ba/ 
5b1(1): 'di khyod kyis shin tu dben par spos la/ yid 'phrog mgum pa la thug pa ma lags par ji lta bur gyur kyang ma stsal cig/ ces de skad cemal bsgo nas/ mchi bya
5b2(1): byas te dmag dpung gi tshogs dang / rol ma'i sgra'i tshogs dang / chas te rang gi yul 'das nas/ ri 'or de dang ha cang yang mi ring ba zhig na shing ldan pa zhig gi drung du
5b3(1): bta pa ste 'dug go/ de'i tshe rgyal po chen po rnam thos kyi bu 'khor gnod sbyin du ma dang / 'khor gnod sbyin brgya phrag du ma dang / 'khor gnod sbyin stong phrag du ma dang / 
5b4(1): 'khor gnod sprin brgya stong phrag du ma dang / lam de ni sa gnod sprin rnams kyi gnod sprin gyi mdun sa ri chas so// de lam de nas chas pa nas/ nam mkha'i lam
5b5(1): la thogs pa ro gyur nas/ de 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gis lam 'di nas lon mang po zhig ta song na bdag gi gzhon pa la na 'ga' yang thogs par ma gyur
5b6(1): na/ gang gis na de ltar thogs par 'di la rgyu ci yod snyam pa las/ des gzhon nu nor bzangs mthong nas/ de 'di ji snyam du sems te/ 'di ni bskal pa bzang po'i/ 
6a1(1): byang chub sems dpa' yin te/ dmag la chas pas nyon mongs par 'gyur gyi 'di'i grogs byas te/ ri 'or ba 'di rnams srog chags
6a2(1): 'ga' la yang gnod par mi 'gyur bar dbab pa snyam du bsams nas/ gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lnga len la smras pa/ lnga len chur shog/ khyod kyis gzhon nu nor bzang
6a3(1): ri 'or ba 'di rnams dang / yul ma bkye bar srog chags 'ga' la yang gnod pa mo bye bar pho bo shig/ gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lnga len gyis bka' bzhin
6a4(1): 'tshal zhes rgyal po rnam thos kyi bra las mnyan nas lha'i dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa/ shing ta la'i tshad tsam gyi skyes pa dang / ri'i tshad tsam gyi glang po che dang / 
6a5(1): glang po che'i tshad tsam gyi shing rta rnams sprul to// de nas ral gri dang / tho ba dang / mda' bo che dang / mdung dang / 'khor lo dang / mdung thung dang / mda' dang / drug
6a6(1): stal sogs ste/ mtshon cha'i khyad par rnam pa sna tshogs dang / sil dkrol gyi sgra rnam pa sna tshogs 'byin pas 'jigs pa chen po ston cing / lnga len mthu chen po'i chog
6b1(1): rnams dang ri 'ong phyin pa dang / glang po che dang / rta dang shing rta'i sgra dang / sil khrol gyis tshogs dang / gnod sbyin rnams kyi rang gi mthu sa rab dag ral bar gyur to/ de nas ri
6b2(1): na gnas pa de rnams kyis dpung gi tshogs de dang ra ba dag ril ba mthong nas mchog tu ngo mtshar skyes te dris pa/ dpung gi tshogs 'di gang nas 'ongs/ de rnams kyis smras pa/ 
6b3(1): myur du sgo phye shig/ gzhon nu nor bzangs 'di'i madrug gnas 'ongs te/ dbang gi tshogs 'don de'i yin no// gal te myur du ma phyen thams cad med par 'gyur ro// de rnams kyis
6b4(1): bdag cag rgya rnams rgyal la mi ldog ste/ gzhon nu blo dang ldan la min/ rgyal po gzhon nu'i tshigs rnams kyis/ bdag cag 'jigs shong skags gyur mad// 
6b5(1): ces smras nas/ de rnams kyi sgo phye ste/ de rnams rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan bsgreng nas bum pa gang ba dang / rol mo'i sgra sna tshogs kyis gzhon nu nero bzangs ba su'o// / 
6b6(1): des kyang dbugs byung nas/ de rnams 'drang ba las sna tshogs sgos te/ dbu thang be cang gnye'u yang bzung de nas ri 'ong ba de rnams pa ba nas/ gzhon nu nor bzangs sla
6b7(1): log go// rgyal po nor can gyis de nyid kyi nub mo'i rmi lam na/ bya rgod cig 'ongs te rgyal po'i lto dral nas rgyu ma bzangs te/ grong khyer de thams cad bskor ba dang / rin po che
7a1(1): sna bdun gyi khyim du 'ongs par mthong ngo // mthong nas de nas rgyal po 'jigs skrag mi dga' zhing spu zing zhes byed nas myung ba myur bar langs te ma
7a2(1): chen po la 'dug nas lag pa 'gram pa la gtad de bzhini 'di las bdag cag rgyal srid las nyams pa'am/ srog gi bar chad du mi 'gyur grang snyam nas sems khongs su chud
7a3(1): cingar 'dug pa las/ de rnams la ngas rmi lam bram ze 'dun na 'don la smras pa dang / des bsams pa la rmi lam de lta bu mthong na ni gdon mi za bar gzhon nus ri bor ba rnams
7a4(1): pham par byas kyi log zhig tu bstan par ba'o snyam nas smras bu/ lha khyod kyis rmi lam du gzigs pa ni/ bzang po ma yin lags te/ gdon ma za bar 'di las lha'i
7a5(1): rgyal srid nyams pa'am/ skrab che'i bar ched du 'gyur lags so/ 'on kyang 'di bzlog pa'i thabs mchis te/ de yang bram ze rnams kyi gsang tshig las mthong ngo // bzlog pa
7a6(1): thabs de ci yin/ lnga skyed mes tshal du brjid dbyigs legs pa tshad la bab pa bgyis la gnas rdo thal gyis byugs ste/ legs par bstar nas/ ri dgas pra mo mang gi khrag gi
7b1(1): bkang la/ de nas lha khrus la gshegs pa na/ rdzing de la them skas gcig las 'jug par bgyi'o// gcig las zhugs nas gnyis pa la 'dzeg par bgyi'o// gnyis pa las zhugs nas
7b2(1): gsum pa la 'dzeg par bgyi'o// gsum pa la zhugs pa nas bzhi pa la 'dzeg pa bgyi'o// de nas bram ze rigs byed dang / rigs byed kyi yan lag gi pha rol tu phyin pa bzhis lha'i zhag
7b3(1): lces bldags la mi ma yin pa'i tshol gi bdug pa bdug go/ de ltar na lnga'i sngon sdig byang zhing yun ring por rgyal srid skyong bar 'gyur ro// rgyal pos smras pa/ de dag thams cad ni
7b4(1): nus 'di ltar ma ming yin pa'i tshil 'di ni shin du dkon no// 'dun na 'don gyis smras pa/ lhang mod pa gang lags pa de dkon lags sam/ rgyal pos smras pa/ de ci lta bu zhig/ 
7b5(1): yin/ mdun na 'don gyis smras pa/ lha 'phrog ma 'di mi 'am ci ma lags sam/ rgyal pos smras pa/ 'dun na 'don 'dil gzhon nu'i srog 'dug gis de ltar ma smra shig
7b6(1): des smras pa/ lha khyim gyi phyir ni 'ga' btang ste/ grong rdal phyir ni khyim btang ngo // yul ljongs phyir ni grong rdal te/ bdag gi phyir nis btang ngo // zhes bgyi ba mi gsan tam/ 
7b7(1): rgyal po bdag nyid brtan gyur nas// gzhon nu blo ldan de la ni// gzhan zhig stsal byed grang gis// yid 'phrog 'di ni gum par mdzod// bdag nyid la mngon par chags pa ni
8a1(1): mi byed pa/ ci yang med pas des khas blangs so// de nas 'dun na 'don gyis ji skad bstan pa bzhin du bya bar brtsams ste/ rdzing brkos
8a2(1): nas rdo thal gyis byugs shing legs par bskur nas/ ri dgas phra mo rnams kyi khrag sogs pa la zhugs so// sbyor ba de nor bzangs kyi btsun mo'o skyes pos shes pas/ 
8a3(1): de rnams dga' ba dang / yid bde ba skyes te bdag lang tshol bab cing gzugs phun sum tshogs pa yin pas ni bdag cag dang / gzhon nu nor bzangs yongs su dga' mgur spyod par
8a4(1): 'gyur ro// zhes de rnams rab tu dga' bar byed pa de dag yid 'phrog pas mthong nas dris pa/ khyod cag ci'i phyir lhag par dga'// ci tsam na gzhan zhig gis yid 'phro go ma/ 
8a5(1): la ji ltar gyur pa rgyas par smra ba dang / yid 'phrog ma sdug bsngal ba dang / yid mi bde ba skyes pa nas/ gzhon nu nor bzangs kyi ma ga na ba der song ste/ rkang pa gnyis la btug
8a6(1): jigs su da ma tha sas pa das smom pa/ gas nyi sa legs pa gas so// ba la sa mag/ la khrug mas gsapa pa la
8b1(1): des brtags na yang bden par mthong nas/ de nas des gtsug ginor pa de dang gos shig yid 'phrog ma la byin nas smras pa/ bum khrod dus la ma bab par ma 'gro zhig/ de lta na kho mo la kham
8b2(1): chu 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro// de nas rgyal pos ji skad bstan pa'i rim pa bzhin du khrus la chas ste/ khrag gis gang ba'i rdzing bur zhugs nas byung ba dang / de nas de rkang pa gnyis bram ze rna
8b3(1): kyis lces paldags so// ji tsam na mi'am ci'i bu mo khrid de shog ces bsgo ba dang / de ma thag kho nar yid 'phrog ma nam mkha' la 'phags te tshigs su bcad de smras pa// bdag
8b4(1): ni reg dang phrad pa dang // bdag ni bdag dang brtses pa las// ba lang mo btags thar lta bu// da ni bdag mo 'gro bar bya// rgyal pos kyang nam mkha'i lam las 'gro ba mthong nas/ 
8b5(1): de skag steng mdun na 'don la smras pa gang gi phyir 'bad par byed pa de ma grub par ma'am ci yid 'brog ma bros so// 'dun na 'don gyis smras pa lha da ni don grub ste/ sngon sdig dang bral lag so// 
8b6(1): de nas yang yid 'brog ma nam mkha'i lam las 'gro ba na/ 'di snyam du sems te/ gang yang bdag gnas skabs 'di thos pa de ni drang srong des bstan pa las gyur gyis/ gal te des
8b7(1): ma bstan na ni bdag bzung zhing 'gro bar mi 'gyur ba zhig/ de lta bas na nges shig drang srong de'i drung du 'gro snyam nas/ de de'i bsti gnas su song ste rkang pa gnyis la phyag byas nas drang srong
9a1(1): pa smras pa/ drang srong chen po khyod kyis bstan pas bdag bzu ste mchis na/ ma'i rig pa rnams thob cing srog gi ba du cha dang rung zhig gis ma gyur to// de bas
9a2(1): gsol ba rig sa te rgya zhig la nor zangs bdag tshol ning mchis ni/ de la bdag gi sor gdubasrel la/ 'di skad ces kyang gsung ba'i rigs so// gzhon du lam yang bgrod dkar ste/ nyon mongs
9a3(1): zung gyigrang ma gyi/ gal te bzlas rdzas sa ma btsun/ de las brdzun pa dgas kyis shi pa'angs yid 'bragams bstan pa byu bugs ni rig pa gsum pa
9a4(1): sa/ de dag rnal pa'i pha rol tan yang gsum mo// de dgargal po'i pha rol na yang mdzes so// de dag rgal ba dang nga'i rgyal po gangs can mchis so// de'i byang phyogs na ri'i rgyal po bur ba'i rtsa/ 
9a5(1): mchis so// de nas lam sgra can dang seng ldeng can dang / rgyud gcig pa dang / rdo rje can dang / 'dod pa'i dgur gyur pa'i gzugs can dang / bur pa'i dbyibs dang / sa srang bu'i dbyibs da / 
9a6(1): tshugal ba dang/ ra nal ci de dag byed kyis nam // rab seng ge can dang / rgyang gcig pa dang / thar pa'i dbyibs lan phyag/ nus 'ju// rdo rje canas bu pa'i rgyal po ga
9a7(1): / thabs 'a dag gis ra ba'i rnam san la bar btu'o/ 'khrul la khang gdod can dang / lug la ba dang / skyes bu srin pa seng su'i gzugs can rig kying gzhom par brtsom/ sa
9b1(1): na sbrul kha chu'i rgyun chen po'i shugs kyis rgyug pa zhig mchis te/ de ni zho shas gzhom par bgyi'o// gang na sbrul ni nag po zhig/ phug na phyed 'dug mthong nas ni/ bdag gi slad du
9b2(1): gzhi gdungs la// mnga' yas bsnun te/ gsad par bgyis// gang na lug gnyis phan tshun nas// brdungs par byed pa mthong na ni// de gnyis rang re bcag brjod dang // lam ni da
9b3(1): par 'gyur lags so// 'jigs tshe skyed mchog thogs pa yi// lcags kyi skyes pa gnyis mthong nas// de gnyis las ni gcig brdegs dang // lam ni rnyed par 'gyur lags so/ 
9b4(1): srin po lcags kyi chu can zhig/ kha 'dzums gdang ba bgyid gzugs na// de tshe de'i dpral ba la// phur pa dag gis gdab par mdzod// de bzhin khron pa klong dag khyil// drug cu'i
9b5(1): khru can la khyod mchongs// sgra mig seng ge ltar ser zhing // ma zad bsnyen par dka' ba'i// gnod sbyin dang ni srin po dag/ gzhu ni bkang ste bsang mdzod la// chu srin 'dzin khros
9b6(1): gang ba yi// chu bo mang pon lnga mdzod cog/ rlungan bye ma leb gdungs dang // sna tshogs dung me da rlung // sbrul can 'dam can gyi klung // nang gnan ni srin mo khro// praM ma le ba dang mam
9b7(1): yin/ gdungs pa nani 'dzin khrim // sna tshogs can 'dadu sbyor gzugs// du ma mi'i mtho'i dran// dag pan na ma'ims// gna'am sbrum ma sprul canan// 'dam can tu
10a1(1): shUl ma li// nang ga la ni brtan bur bya// phye ma lebal rtul pong bya// gdung bar 'dzin khri kha bcing ngo // sna tshogs can du klu sna tshogs// dud mo can du yin
10a2(1): bde bas// dgod byed du ni mi smra ba'i// sbyor bas kun tu brgal bar mdzod// sbrul can du ni sbrul bdug gi/ sngags kyi sbyor dang 'od ma can// klung du mchor rnon gda' ba yi// 
10a3(1): sbyor bas kun tu rgal ba'i mdzod// chu rnams rgal na saM btsag gnas na// gon da sbyin lnga brgya yod pa de// rnams la sran tshugs gzhom mdzad cig/ de nas ni mi'am ci'i
10a4(1): rgyal po'i pheM brang mchis so// zhes gsung zhig/ drang srong de la yid 'phrog mas de skad ces smras nas// rkang pa gnyis la mgo bos btags te song ngo // ci tsam na gzhon nu no
10a5(1): bzangs kyi ri 'or de phab nas skyes khyer te glang po'i grong khyer du 'ongs so// zhes rgyal pos thos nas/ mchog tu dga' ba skyes so// de nas gzhon nu ngal sos nas pa'i drung du song
10a6(1): ste/ phyag byas mdun du 'dug pa dang / rgyal pos mchog tu dga' bar 'gyur ba'i gtam byas nas smras pa/ gzhon nu khyed bde bar 'ongs sam/ lha khrod kyis bka' drin gyis
10a7(1): 'bab ste ste'u bzung nas sna bo skas lags te dpra dang skyes kyang 'di dag lags kyis phyag mdzod du gzhug tu gsol/ rgyal pos smras pa/ bu legs par byas kyis ban
10b1(1): so// de nas gzhon nus pa la phyag byas nas chas pa dang / rgyal pos smras pa/ gzhon nu skyes la lhan cig kho nar longs spyod kyis 'dug shig/ lha bdag gis yid 'phrog ma
10b2(1): mthong nas yun ring du zhig legs pas mchi'o lags so// gzhon nu deng 'gro ba shol la sang song shig/ de gal chung zhing 'di skad ces smras so// yab nges par deng nyid badrag ma
10b3(1): lags so// rgyal po cang mi smra bar 'dug go/ de nas gzhon nu rang gi khyim du song bas/ btsun mo pho brang gi sgo dpal kyang stong par mthong ba nas/ de sems khongs su chud bzhin du
10b4(1): zhugs na/ yid 'phrog ma ma mthong nas snying stor to/ phan tshun du rgyu zhing yid 'brog ma zhes spu byung ngo // ci tsam na btsun mo rnams 'tshogs nas/ btsun mo de rnams kyi ga
10b5(1): glung bskur ba dang / de'i snying la gzug rngus gzug pas yang nas yang du dris pa las/ de rnams kyis ji ltar gyur pa smras so// de mya ngan las yod klong bar gyur te/ bud med de rnams kyis
10b6(1): swA pa/ lha btsun mo'i 'khor 'di ni/ de bas bud med shin tu khyad par 'phags pa dag mchis na/ ci'i slad thugs ngan mdzad/ des snying rje med cing byas pa chud son pa thob nas ma'i
10b7(1): drung du song ste/ rkang pa la gtags nas smras pa/ yum yid bzhin yon tan ldan gyur cig/ gzugs mdzes phun sum tshogs pa yi// yid 'phrog ma ni mi 'da' na// bdag gi yid
11a1(1): 'phrog gang du mchis// yid kyis rab tu brgyags snyam na'ang // bdag gi yid ni kun tu rmongs// de dang bral bar gyur pa yi// snying ni shin tu gdungs pa nyid
11a2(1): bdag gi yid du che zhing yid 'phrog la// yid du 'thad cing yid la dga' ba yi// bdag nyid sdug bsngal 'di ni gang gnas mchis// des smras pa bu ying 'phrog ma sdug bsngal mi zad pa
11a3(1): nyamang bar gyur nas kho mos btang ngo // yum ji ltar gyur pa/ des ji ltar gyur pa thams cad rgyas par smras pa dang / nges pa snying rje med cing byas pa mi bzo ba yin no zhes smras nas smras
11a4(1): pa/ yum gang du mchis pa/ shul ni gang nas des smras pa gang du yid 'phrog song ba yi/ lam der dang drang srong dang / seng ge dag gis brtag brten cing / chos kyi rgyal po gnas pa yin
11a5(1): de yid 'phrog ma dang bral ba'i sdug bsngal gyis mi bzad par nyams thag cing snying rje'i skad du bla zhing smre sngags 'don pa/ yid bzhin yon tan ldan pa gyur pa'i// yid 'phrog ma ni mi
11a6(1): 'da' na// zhes bya ba nas bdag gi sdug bsngal 'di ni gang nas 'ongs zhes bya ba'i bar gong ma bzhin no// de nas mas smras pa/ bu btsun ma'i 'khor 'di na de bas ches khyad par du
11a7(1): 'phags pa'i bud med dag yod na/ ci'i phyir mya ngan byed/ gzhon nus smras pa/ yum de ma rnyed par bdag dga' bar ga la 'gyur/ des de dbugs phyung yang 'on kyang mngon gyis
11b1(1): gdungs nas de'i khungs tshol zhing phan tshun du btsal bar brtsams te/ de'i blo skyes pa/ gang kho nas thob pa de nyid la re shig dri'o snyam nas des sngon pa spang leb car gyi drung du song ste dris
11b2(1): pa khyod kyis yid 'phrog ma gang nas rnyed des smras pa/ ri bo che ge mo'i nges la drang srong zhig gnas te/ de'i bskyi ga nas na tshangs pa 'du ba zhes bgyi ba'i rdzing mchis te/ der khrus la
11b3(1): zhugs pa las/ drang srong gi bstan nas rnyed de// des bsams pa/ da ni drang srong song dang / de las khungs phyin par 'gyur ro snyam mo// rgyal pos gzhon nu ni yid 'phrog ma dang bral
11b4(1): bas shin tu yid blong ba'i gtam thos so// de nas rgyal pos smras pa/ gzhon nu khyod yid blong du ci yong / da ni de bas khyad par du 'phags pa'i chung ma byin no// des smras pa/ yab
11b5(1): bdag ga ni de ma lags pa'i mchis brang gi 'khor dang mchis par rje mi thogs lags so// rgyal pos de la lam du ma smras kyang ma zlogs so// de nas rgyal pos grong khyer gyi sgo/ 
11b6(1): dang / ra ba'i khar ci nas kyang gzhon nu phyir mi tshor bar bya ba'i phyir skyes bu srungs ma dag bkod do// de nas gzhan nu ni mtshan thogs thag mi nyal bar gyur to// lnga po 'di dag ni
11b7(1): mtshan mo cung zad nyal gyi phal cher mi nyal te/ lnga gang zho na skyes bu bud med la chags pas sems bcings pa dang / bud med skyes pa la chags pa dang / srog chags drang ba dang / 
12a1(1): chom rkun pa'i rab bgo ba dang / dge slong brtson 'grus brtsams pa yin no zhes gsungs so// de nas gzhon nu 'di snyam du sems te/ gal te bdag
12a2(1): sgo nas song la rgyal po'i sgo spangs kyi srungs ma gtum po dag yod do// de rnams kyis bdag chad par gcod pa 'am/ srog dang bral bar byed par 'gyur gyis/ ci nas kyang bdag
12a3(1): srungs ma med pa'i lam nas 'gro ba snyam du/ de mtshan mo langs te ut+pal sngon po'i rtsibs mgo bcings pa'i 'phreng ba rgyal mtshan la btags nas gang na srungs ma'i mi med pa
12a4(1): de nas babs pa ni zla ba shar to// de nas des zla ba la bltas nas/ yid 'brogs ma dang bral ba'i smre sngags 'di lta bu dag 'don par byed de/ zla ba nya rgyu skar rgyal po mtshan mo
12a5(1): gsal mdzad kyi// khyod kyi snar ma'i mig tu sdug pa sde dpon bzang // bdag gi sdug pa ut+pal lta bu'i mig/ yid 'brog ces bgyi khyod kyis sa stengs gzigs legs sam
12a6(1): zhes smras na/ sngon gyi dga' ba nyams su myong ba dran zhing ba las// ri dgas mo zhig mthong nas de la yang smras pa// kye ma ri dgas mo khyod phra chu lo ma za// khyod ni legs kyu
12a7(1): bde sbyor bdag ni rngon pa min// ri dgas mo ltar mig skyes ring bas gzugs bzang // bdag gi yid 'phrog ces bya khyod kyis mthong gyur tam// de nas song ste phyogs gzhan du
12b1(1): phyin pa dang / tshal me tog 'bras bus mdzes par byas pa'i snying po la bung bdag longs spyod pa mthong nas/ de nas bung ba bzhin la smras pa/ sbrang dri'i bung ba ri bo mthong mthing lta bu
12b2(1): mdog spyugs ma'i dbubs dang pad+ma dag la gnas 'cha' ba// skra'i tshogs ring kha dog bung bltar gnag pa// bdag gi yi 'i 'phrog ces bya khyod kyis mthong gyur tam/ 
12b3(1): phyogs de na sa kyang song ba dang / sbrul zhig mthong ngo // mthong nas kyang smras pa/ kye ma sbrul nag shing lo lta bur lce g.yo zhing // mig dang kha'i nang nas dud pa'i tshogs 'byin pa
12b4(1): khyod kyi gdug pa'i me dang 'dod chag sa mer mi tshungs// bdag gi yid 'phrog ces bya khyod kyis mthong gyur tam/ de nas kyang phyogs gzhan zhig tu song ba dang / tshal gzhan zhig na/ 
12b5(1): khwa byug sgra 'byin pa zhig mthong ngakaN+Da mthong nas kyang khu byug de la yang smras pa/ kye ma khu byug tshal mchog ldan shing la gnas la// 'dab rags tshogs kyi rgyal po yid 'phrog pa
12b6(1): ut+pal sngon po lta bung dri zhim mdzes pa'i mig/ bdag gi yid 'brog ces bya khyod kyis mthong gyur tam// phyogs de nas kyang song ba dang / shing mya ngan tshal zhes bya ba me tog thas
12b7(1): cad rgyas pa zhig mthong nas/ ming gi rnam grangs bkra shis zhes brjod pa// ldan pa rnams kyi rgyal po cher gyung pa// yid 'phrog mya ngan gyis ni blong bdag/ thal mo sbyar na khyod
13a1(1): kyis mya ngon songs// de de ltar yid blong bzhin rim gyis drang song de'i bsti gnas su phyin nas des drang srong de la dul ba dang bcas pas phyag byas nas/ 
13a2(1): smras pa/ bzo 'bags gos sra shing shun dang ni g.yang gzhi bsnams// rtsa ba myu gu N+ya ru bil ba ka bi gsol// drang srong mgos btung phyag 'tshal bdag gi yid 'phrog ma// khyed
13a3(1): kyis gzigs sam khyod kyis bdag la myur du gsungs/ de nas drang srong des gzhon nu nor bzangs la/ byon pa legs so zhes bya ba dang / stan gting ba la sogs pa sngar bya ba'i yang dag par
13a4(1): dga' bar byas nas smras pa/ smin ma 'jam pa'i smin btsugs mthon mthing bzhin legs mthong na dga' ba'i gzugs 'chang ba/ bzhin ras zla ba nye 'dra ut+pal sngon po lta bu'i mig de bdag gi
13a5(1): mthong / dpon khyod bge rkyongs bzhugs te rtsa ba 'bras bu sna tshogs gsol mdzod cig/ slad kyis bde blag byin 'gyur 'dil bdag gi yid la the tshom yongs ma mchis// smin ma bzang pos 'di skad
13a6(1): tshig smras te/ gzhon nu khyod la sred pas bag mi bde// nags khrod gnas pa'ang sdug bsngal chen po ste// gshegs par gyur na nges par bdag gzhag mthong // des sor thub rgya 'di byin nas
13a7(1): smras pa// lam yang sa la dgrod dka' bas nyon mongs par 'gyur gyis sar log shig/ gal te bzlog kyang 'dug tu ma btab na/ de la ma bstan pa'i rigs so// des yang 'di skad ces bstan
13b1(1): te/ byang phyogs logs na ri nag po gsum yod do// de dag rgal ba dang / ri 'or ba rgyal po gangs can zhes bya ba yod de phyogs de nas/ sman 'di dag blangs par bya ste/ 'di lta ste/ shin tu'o ma
13b2(1): 'dzag ces bya ba'i sman yod de/ de mar las btsos nas btang bar bya'o// des na skom pa dang bkres pa med cing dran pa dang mthu stobs 'phel bar gyur/ spre'u zhig kying bkri bar bya gsang sngag
13b3(1): kyang bslab par bya// gzhu mnga' dang bcas pa dang nor bu 'o dang ldan pa dang / dug gsod pa sman dug sel ba dang / lcags kyi bur ba gsum dang ldan pa/ bra la ra yang bcang bar bya'o// ri'i rgyal
13b4(1): po gangs can gyi byang phyogs na/ ri'i phur pa'i rtse yod do// de nas lam chu sgra can dang / seng ge can dang / rgyud gcig pa dang / rdo rje can dang / 'dod dgung sgyur ba'i gzugs can dang / phung ba'i
13b5(1): dbyibs dang / sa srung bu'i dbyibs dang / mi g.yo ba dang / rab grol lo// khyod kyis ri de dag rgal dgos te/ de la ri bo sor ldeng can la ni/ phug nas 'jug/ rgyad gcig pa dang / phur pa'i dbying
13b6(1): la yang phug pas 'jug/ rdo rje can la ni bya'i rgyal pos 'jug ste/ thabs 'di dag gis ri bo de rnams rgal bar bya'o// 'khrul 'khor ra gdong can dang / lug lta bu dang / skyes bu ser skya'i
13b7(1): gzugs can dag gzhom par bya'o// bu ga ne sbrul kha chu'i rgyun chen po'i shugs kyis rgyug ba zhig mchis te/ de ni zho shas gzhom par bya'o// yang na sbrul ne nag po zhig/ phug na phyed 'dug
14a1(1): mthong nas ni/ bdag gi slad du gzhu gdungs la// mda' yis bsnun te bsad par gyis/ gang na lugs gnyis phan tshun nas/ gdung bar byed pa mthong ba ni/ 
14a2(1): de gnyis ra re ba cag mdzod dang // lam ni rnyed par 'gyur lags so// 'jigs pa chen po mtshon thogs pa'i// lcags kyi skyes bu gnyis mthong nas// de gnyis las gcig brdegs pa
14a3(1): dang /  lam ni rnyed par 'gyur legs so// srin mo lcags kyi mchu can zhig/ kha 'dzums gdangs pa bgyid gzigs nas// de'i tshe de'i dpral ba la// phur pa gang gis gdab par mdzod// 
14a4(1): de bzhin khron pa glong khrag 'khyil// drug cu'i khru can la khyod chongs// skra mig seng ge ltar ser zhing // mi bzad bsnyen par dka' ba yi// gnod sbyin dang ni srin po dag/ gzhu ba kang ste ni bsad
14a5(1): mdzod la/ chu srin 'dzan khris gang ba yi// chu bo mang ba rgal mdzod cig/ nang ga phye ma leb gdungs dang // sna tshogs dud mo rgod pa dang // sbrul can 'od ma can gyi klung // na ga na ni srin ma
14a6(1): khro// phye ma leb gdungs ma ma yin// gdungs pa na ni 'dzin khri mang // sna tshogs can na 'dod dgur gzugs// dud mor ma 'am ci'i bran// de god pa na ni mi'am ci// mna' ma sbrul mang sprul
14a7(1): canan// 'dod ma can klung shal ma li// ning ga la ni bstan par bya// phye ma leb la rtul pad bya// gdung bar 'dzin khri kha bcing ngo // sna tshogs can du klu sna tshogs// dud mo can du yid no/ 
14b1(1): 'debs// dgod byed du ni mi smra ba'i// stor bas kun tu rgal bar mdzod// sbrul can na ni sbrul gdug gi/ sngags kyi sbyong dang 'ong ba can// klung du mchon rngon gdab pa yi// sbyar bas
14b2(1): kun tu rgal bar mdzod// chu bo rnams rgal nas gcan pa'i gnas na gnod sbyin lnga brgya yang ba de rnams la sran tshugs te gzhom par mdzod cig/ de nas ni mi'am ci'i rgyal po'i pho brang
14b3(1): mchis so// zhes gsungs shig/ de nas gzhon nu nor bzangs kyis ji skad bstan pa'i sman dang / gsang sngags dang / sman dug sel gyi sbyong ba rnams btsal ba'i phyir/ drang srong de'i
14b4(1): rkang pa la lan mang du phyag byas nas song ngo // de nas des spre'u ma btogs par ji skad bstan pa thams cad sta gon byas nas/ de nas de rnams khyer te yang drang srong de'i drung du song ba dang / 
14b5(1): des de la spre'u byin nas smras pa/ gzhon nu 'bad pa 'di ts+tshi bya/ yid 'phrog ma ni ci zhig dgos// khyod ni gcig bu grogs med pa// lus gnon za bar 'gyur gyis mthong / gzhon nus
14b6(1): smras pa/ drang srong chen po bdag ni gdon ma za bar mchi'o// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ mkha' la zla ba rgya ba grogs shing dka' la mchis// mche ba'i mthu stobs ldan pa'i ri dgas gtso bo dang / 
14b7(1): me yas nags sreg pa na grogs shig ga la mchis// bdag lta bu la grogs pa mthu ldan ci zhig 'tshal/ kye ci rgya mtshor chur 'jug par mi bgyi'am ci lags sbrul bgyis zin ces gsol gru

15a3(1): rgyal bar byas nas ma'i'am ci'i rgyal po ljon pa'i grong khyer dang nye ba zhig du song ba dang / gzhon nus grong khyer dpal dang ldan pa/ skyes mos chel me tog dang / 'bras bu sna tsheg sa reng
15a4(1): ldan pas mdzes pas byas pa/ bya sna tshogs kyis snyan pa/ rdzing bu dang mtshe'u ring po dang gru bzhi dang / mI'am ci mo rnams kyis bskor ba de la/ ma 'am ci mo rnams chu len du 'ong
15a5(1): pa mthong nas gzhon nu ner bzangs kyis de rnams la smras pa/ chu mang pos ci zhig bya/ de rnams kyi saM smras pa/ mi 'am ci'i rgyal po ldan pa'i sras me yid 'phrog ma zhes bgyi

15a7(1): blugs sam/ 'on te rim gyis de rnams kyis smras pa/ rim gyis so// des bsams pa thabs 'di bzang ste/ sor gdub kyi rgya 'di dgos bum pa gcig gi nang du gzhug go// 
15b1(1): snyam nas/ des mi'am ci mo gcig gis bum par mi tshor bang bcug nas/ mi'am tsamo de la smras pa/ khyod kyis bum pa 'dis thog mar yid 'phrog ma la khrus byos shig
15b2(1): des bsams pa/ gdon mi za bar 'di la dgras pa zhig yod par 'gyur ro snyam nas/ de nas des brim pa de thog ma yid 'phrog ma'i spyi bor lhug pa las ci tsam na sor gdub kyi
15b3(1): rgya par du lhung ba dang / yid 'phrog ma sa de 'bregs so// de nas mi 'am ci mo la dris pa 'dir mi 'ga' zhig ma 'ongs sam/ des smos pa mchis so// song la de dben pa
15b4(1): zhig tu zhog cig/ des de nang du khrid nas dben pa zhig tu gzhag go/ de nas yid 'phrog mas pa'i rkang pa gnyis la gtugs te smras pa/ ya ba gal te bdag gi khyim/ 
15b5(1): tha ba gyid pa/ gzhon nu nor bzangs de mchis na de la khyod kyis ci zhig bgyi/ des smras pa/ 'di ma yin te/ cir yang mi mkho bas/ ngas de dum bu brgyar byas la phyog

15b7(1): nas dkris dang bral te/ kun nas dkris pa dang bral nas smras pa/ gal te gzhan nu de 'ongs na/ ngas khyed rgyan thams cad brgyan la nor dang yo byad mang po dang ma'am tso mo stong gis

100a6(1): yin snyam na/ khyod kyis de ltar mi lta ste/ 'on kyang de'i tshe de'i dus na khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin 'di nyid yin no// de'i 'og tu bskal pa bzang po 'di nyid la skye dgu tshe le nyi khri thub pa na yang dag par rdzogs

100b4(1): na med pa lnga dang ma rnams kyi ston pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ston pa gang 'jig rten du byung nas ngas 'khor stong nyis bcwa lnga bcu dang / phyogs 'dir gshegs pa na/ da ltar yang khyim bdag mgon med zas skyon gyis smon
